class="Header--left--x8TGxDL"><span class="Header--updateTime--YXGPhcZ">更新时间：2025-09-25 10:09:20</span></div><div class="Header--right--l4TSW1E"><div class="Header--linkButton--LpCRs1O"><div <main id="main-2851847"><p id="660a5d32b2vga" data-tag="shortdesc" class="shortdesc">本文介绍语音合成<span class="help-letter-space"></span>CosyVoice Java SDK<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的参数和接口细节。</p><div data-tag="body" class="body"><section id="baf59c3e71j7r" class="section"><section id="b7cdf88b2bcv0" props="china" data-cond-props="china" class="section"><p id="8f92514f157fy"><b>用户指南：</b>关于模型介绍和选型建议请参见<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/text-to-speech" id="a80aa4cb2fod0" title="" class="xref">语音合成-CosyVoice/Sambert</a>。</p><p id="c765dbfec7mv4"><b>在线体验</b>：仅<span class="help-letter-space"></span>cosyvoice-v1<span class="help-letter-space"></span>支持<a class="" href="https://bailian.console.aliyun.com/#/efm/model_experience_center/voice?currentTab=voiceTts" id="899b0b0fd6c4t">在线体验</a>。</p></section></section><section id="7ffab42f128aq" class="section"><h2 id="7b437379e66yg"><b>前提条件</b></h2><section id="9b6cf7c77c8cd" docid="5220136" is-conref="true" class="section"><ul id="031bf73ae2800" sourcekey="2000000000106"><li id="bd76aa7469ww3" sourcekey="2000000000108"><section id="29882aaeda6lb" sourcekey="2000000000110" class="section"><p id="52a05b0974e88">已开通服务并<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/get-api-key" id="e7adb2811c5ue" title="" class="xref">获取<span class="help-letter-space"></span>API Key</a>。请<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/configure-api-key-through-environment-variables" id="f09e217b2ers2" title="" class="xref">配置<span class="help-letter-space"></span>API Key<span class="help-letter-space"></span>到环境变量</a>，而非硬编码在代码中，防范因代码泄露导致的安全风险。</p><div id="8e1399fe65goe" type="note" class="note note-note"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note note"></i><strong>说明 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><p jc="start" id="ab844f386ejq8" style="text-align:start">当您需要为第三方应用或用户提供临时访问权限，或者希望严格控制敏感数据访问、删除等高风险操作时，建议使用<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/generate-temporary-api-key" id="b696e62d73gmi" title="" class="xref">临时鉴权<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Token</a>。</p><p id="78827e82c9sms">与长期有效的 API Key 相比，临时鉴权 Token 具备时效性短（60<span class="help-letter-space"></span>秒）、安全性高的特点，适用于临时调用场景，能有效降低<span class="help-letter-space"></span>API Key<span class="help-letter-space"></span>泄露的风险。</p><p data-spm-anchor-id="395e44f7.4d3ad9aa.0.i169.75273d33lusyIA" jc="start" id="4cf1be0949hy9" style="text-align:start">使用方式：在代码中，将原本用于鉴权的 API Key 替换为获取到的临时鉴权 Token 即可。</p></div></div></section></li><li id="5be7a83b30p5l" sourcekey="2000000000123"><p id="4c2a4fe88b68f"><a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/install-sdk" id="1ffb446a9b89a" title="" class="xref">安装最新版<span class="help-letter-space"></span>DashScope SDK</a>。</p></li></ul></section></section><section id="aab5537486ib4" class="section"><h2 jc="left" id="c86fb378canso" style="text-align:left"><b>模型与价格</b></h2><section id="fca81bf591qfo" 平衡质量与价格，其余版本仅建议在兼容或低要求场景使用。</p><div class="table-wrapper"><table class="fixed-table" style="width: 622px; visibility: hidden; top: 39px;"><colgroup colwidth="0.52*" class="help-letter-space"></span>个字符，英文、标点符号、空格均按照<span class="help-letter-space"></span>1<span class="help-letter-space"></span>个字符计费</p></section><p id="a3db25e25458n">更多说明：<span data-tag="ph" id="fc6d1f9865ipo" props="china" data-cond-props="china" class="ph"><a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/rate-limit#95cc317401h9u" id="f87401e066z1y" title="" class="xref">限流</a>、<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/text-to-speech#6d9a0ce4f90vx" id="85fda3f1f8kf1" title="" class="xref">功能特性</a></span></p></section></section><section id="003ae2f693czy" class="section"><h2 id="763d3a16a8mpb"><b>语音合成文本限制与格式规范</b></h2><section id="a896b45529gui" class="section"><h3 id="ee3f013b84pp2"><b>文本长度限制</b></h3><ul id="5d9c09f059rqt"><li id="f82c93b37cgsb"><p id="409fa990cdim4" data-init-id="a3c0acfaa2sur">非流式调用（<a href="#82d9324616ifx" id="3948e6a58edmi" title="" class="xref">同步调用</a>、<a href="#cc2a504f344s2" id="74fa9afc75y65" title="" class="xref">异步调用</a>或<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>非流式调用）：单次发送文本长度不得超过 2000 字符。</p></li><li id="63e07799240px"><p id="d6b12fb100opz">流式调用（<a href="#ba023aacfbr84" id="8abcbbde6fnwt" title="" class="xref">流式调用</a>或<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>流式调用）：单次发送文本长度不得超过 2000 字符，且累计发送文本总长度不得超过 20 万字符。</p></li></ul></section><section id="3517bae321stx" class="section"><section id="fe610789fd9ug" class="section"><h3 uuid="malx3ogvdo40vezglsv" id="37d964dceaz3i" data-init-id="8e224313302ft"><b>字符计算规则</b></h3><ul id="9ed1a966562eo"><li id="3a2a691ba1jvj"><p id="ce4c1cad2ceet">汉字：2<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li><li id="cbe18841cfz41"><p id="546dc28ff5rkl">英文字母/数字/标点/空格：1<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li><li id="56d1191f1d6xa"><p id="8d92a00d18446">计算文本长度时，SSML<span class="help-letter-space"></span>标签内容也包含在内</p></li><li id="744361ff49oam"><p id="5d75df4b17qqj">示例：</p><ul id="b74768784d2ka"><li id="4c3896be95q1r"><p id="d4f5b6b47ez8u"><code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="d606cb7f53mgh">"你好"</code>&nbsp;→ 2+2=4<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li><li id="1b55810489x1s"><p id="320918a0863g7"><code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="4c434e77b6n6m">"中<span class="help-letter-space"></span>A<span class="help-letter-space"></span>文<span class="help-letter-space"></span>123"</code>&nbsp;→ 2+1+2+1+1+1=8<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li><li id="29eb4d8734yp4"><p id="ec9fb1b13ejsu"><code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="62e390a28d0fe">"中文。"</code>&nbsp;→ 2+2+1=5<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li><li id="975f5145f6bcz"><p id="1fbc1fea1axpv"><code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="8161212399zw1">"中 文。"</code>&nbsp;→ 2+1+2+1=6<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li><li id="8b539becf41u3"><p id="5f7e6d3e97gyv"><code data-tag="code" id="88f5c97007nro" class="code">"&lt;speak&gt;你好&lt;speak/&gt;"</code>&nbsp;→ 7+2+2+8=19<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符</p></li></ul></li></ul></section><section id="b5f854a8152hn" class="section"><h3 id="bcae611014vy2"><b>编码格式</b></h3><p id="260de778c9yp6">需采用<span class="help-letter-space"></span>UTF-8<span class="help-letter-space"></span>编码。</p></section><section id="c1e0978d838x3" class="section"><h3 id="8f5fca598cx7t"><b>数学表达式支持说明</b></h3><p id="7d0d39673998e">当前数学表达式解析功能仅适用于<code data-tag="code" id="09ca6b6ca6qfg" class="code">cosyvoice-v2</code>模型，支持识别中小学常见的数学表达式，包括但不限于基础运算、代数、几何等内容。</p><p id="7730c74784our">详情请参见<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/latex-capability-support-description" id="1c5b42833d6w8" title="" class="xref">Latex<span class="help-letter-space"></span>能力支持说明</a>。</p></section></section><section id="a92a0cf604vzd" class="section"><h3 id="99f13f3817ptm"><a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/introduction-to-cosyvoice-ssml-markup-language" id="a51573b4753ag" title="" class="xref">SSML</a><span class="help-letter-space"></span><b>标记语言支持说明</b></h3><p id="01d7a20146qod">当前<span class="help-letter-space"></span>SSML（Speech Synthesis Markup Language，语音合成标记语言）功能仅适用于<code data-tag="code" id="f479f440b6vt4" data-init-id="09ca6b6ca6qfg" class="code">cosyvoice-v2</code>模型，使用时需满足以下条件：</p><ul id="871f3159b6uwc"><li id="deaa14fdb0o6a"><p id="fe966b6069irm">使用<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/install-sdk" id="0432ae17cbota" title="" class="xref">DashScope SDK</a>&nbsp;2.20.3 或更高版本</p></li><li id="1a7eadb5004nt"><p id="ec7949fca55a9">仅支持<a href="#82d9324616ifx" id="e6f691141frso" title="" class="xref">同步调用</a>和<a href="#cc2a504f344s2" id="60901d8ce04hh" title="" class="xref">异步调用</a>（即<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="4ea0fb152ehu3" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="5f8b2612fa9tm" class="code">call</code>方法），不支持<a href="#ba023aacfbr84" id="29d00cc6e4zlk" title="" class="xref">流式调用</a>（即<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="98a6acbc245t0" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="290305da714kf" data-init-id="5f8b2612fa9tm" class="code">streamingCall</code>方法）和<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#b0f81fef83ojo" id="d84b38b39doog" title="" class="xref">Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>调用</a>。</p></li><li id="3536854053lhi"><p id="c9af63d3b8i72">使用方法与普通语音合成一致：将包含<span class="help-letter-space"></span>SSML<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的文本传入<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="b97acf6f4fm15" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="3867bc2491ueb" data-init-id="5f8b2612fa9tm" class="code">call</code>方法即可</p></li></ul></section></section><section id="7fbe895f7ffvb" class="section"><h2 id="6bc2d05715bdk"><b>快速开始</b></h2><p jc="left" id="6c8eedfd8e9rb" style="text-align:left"><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="4d2ef7853d82s" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>提供了语音合成的关键接口，支持以下几种调用方式：</p><ul id="b8acd4a26fonp"><li id="98c820d9e8t9q"><p id="42d1bfe5ad3id">同步调用：提交文本后，服务端立即处理并返回完整的语音合成结果。整个过程是阻塞式的，客户端需要等待服务端完成处理后才能继续下一步操作。适合短文本语音合成场景。</p></li><li id="a46c28b461wqd"><p id="5a9dff776bxjc">异步调用：将文本一次发送至服务端并实时接收语音合成结果，不允许将文本分段发送。适用于对实时性要求高的短文本语音合成场景。</p></li><li id="03c0eae4b6p02"><p id="ac6e28b413x3f">流式调用：将文本逐步发送到服务端并实时接收语音合成结果，允许将长文本分段发送，服务端在接收到部分文本后便立即开始处理。适合实时性要求高的长文本语音合成场景。</p></li></ul><section id="881157aa56lll" class="section"><h3 id="82d9324616ifx"><b>同步调用</b></h3><p id="2ce86f5e87eii">同步提交语音合成任务，直接获取完整结果。</p><hetu type="flowchart" id="5893a7ef21uvn" versionid="CAEQURiBgIDHpsn4phkiIDQ0ZGE2OTk3NmY5NTRhNDVhZDQwNWE3ZGZiMzk4Yjk5" uuid="4709861_20241015153444.149" hetuid="06bafae3-3ef7-4826-827a-f3b7ee11c684"><img src="https://help-static-aliyun-doc.aliyuncs.com/assets/img/zh-CN/9516678571/CAEQURiBgIDHpsn4phkiIDQ0ZGE2OTk3NmY5NTRhNDVhZDQwNWE3ZGZiMzk4Yjk54709861_20241015153444.149.svg" alt="image" class="image break flowchart hetu" loading="lazy"></hetu><p id="be464cdad1dxr">实例化<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="94305e34e3d8e" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>绑定<a href="#a96bfa6340jdd" id="7fc5d07a30y22" title="" class="xref">请求参数</a>，调用<code data-tag="code" id="859bbfcea5vy9" class="code">call</code>方法进行合成并获取二进制音频数据。</p><p id="db97137d2a9fq">发送的文本长度不得超过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>2000<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符（详情请参见<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="ebdd4bbbc8dzl" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="747093619d215" data-init-id="5f8b2612fa9tm" class="code">call</code>方法）。</p><div type="important" id="9a9cf86f740vw" class="note note-important"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note important"></i><strong>重要 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><p id="75e6048b1a46f">每次调用<code data-tag="code" id="b59db2676a478" class="code">call</code>方法前，需要重新初始化<code data-tag="code" id="3e176386c123r" class="code">SpeechSynthesizer</code>实例。</p></div></div>
    <section class="collapse" id="e870bf51f2gl1">
      <div class="expandable-title-bold">
        <span class="title"><p id="b9ed62e89fmlz" data-tag="expandable-title" class="expandable-title"><b>点击查看完整示例</b></p></span>
        <i class="icon help-iconfont help-icon-zhankai1 smallFont"></i>
      </div>
      <div class="expandable-content">

    <div class="help-code-block">

      <pre code-type="xCode" id="66d4a888c5bl7" data-tag="codeblock" outputclass="language-java" class="pre codeblock language-java"><code data-highlighted="yes" class="hljs language-java"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesisParam;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesizer;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.io.File;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.io.FileOutputStream;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.io.IOException;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.nio.ByteBuffer;

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Main</span> {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 模型</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">model</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"cosyvoice-v2"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 音色</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">voice</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"longxiaochun_v2"</span>;

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">streamAudioDataToSpeaker</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 请求参数</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesisParam</span> <span class="hljs-variable">param</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span>
                SpeechSynthesisParam.builder()
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// 若没有将API Key配置到环境变量中，需将下面这行代码注释放开，并将your-api-key替换为自己的API Key</span>
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// .apiKey("your-api-key")</span>
                        .model(model) <span class="hljs-comment">// 模型</span>
                        .voice(voice) <span class="hljs-comment">// 音色</span>
                        .build();

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 同步模式：禁用回调（第二个参数为null）</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesizer</span> <span class="hljs-variable">synthesizer</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">SpeechSynthesizer</span>(param, <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);
        <span class="hljs-type">ByteBuffer</span> <span class="hljs-variable">audio</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>;
        <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 阻塞直至音频返回</span>
            audio = synthesizer.call(<span class="hljs-string">"今天天气怎么样？"</span>);
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception e) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RuntimeException</span>(e);
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">finally</span> {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 任务结束关闭websocket连接</span>
            synthesizer.getDuplexApi().close(<span class="hljs-number">1000</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"bye"</span>);
        }
        <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (audio != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 将音频数据保存到本地文件“output.mp3”中</span>
            <span class="hljs-type">File</span> <span class="hljs-variable">file</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">File</span>(<span class="hljs-string">"output.mp3"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 首次发送文本时需建立 WebSocket 连接，因此首包延迟会包含连接建立的耗时</span>
            System.out.println(
                    <span class="hljs-string">"[Metric] requestId为："</span>
                            + synthesizer.getLastRequestId()
                            + <span class="hljs-string">"首包延迟（毫秒）为："</span>
                            + synthesizer.getFirstPackageDelay());
            <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> (<span class="hljs-type">FileOutputStream</span> <span class="hljs-variable">fos</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">FileOutputStream</span>(file)) {
                fos.write(audio.array());
            } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (IOException e) {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RuntimeException</span>(e);
            }
        }
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">(String[] args)</span> {
        streamAudioDataToSpeaker();
        System.exit(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    }
}</code></pre>

  </section><section id="cb409d157f0lk" class="section"><h3 id="cc2a504f344s2"><b>异步调用</b></h3><p id="a79539143d603">异步提交语音合成任务，通过注册<code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="7db373188f98o">ResultCallback</code>回调，逐帧接收实时语音分段数据。</p><hetu type="flowchart" id="8d7647e9bfc86" versionid="CAEQVRiBgMCfo..hrBkiIGEyMjNkZjVlMWZiYzRhZDU4ZjEyZjdjMmMzYjM1YzMz" uuid="4709861_20241015153444.149" hetuid="5360fd0d-b0c2-40af-afa1-9cbbad8ed8bb"><img src="https://help-static-aliyun-doc.aliyuncs.com/assets/img/zh-CN/9516678571/CAEQVRiBgMCfo..hrBkiIGEyMjNkZjVlMWZiYzRhZDU4ZjEyZjdjMmMzYjM1YzMz4709861_20241015153444.149.svg" alt="image" class="image break flowchart hetu" loading="lazy"></hetu><p id="11ff29f8199zy">实例化<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="d48116a334sdj" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>绑定<a href="#a96bfa6340jdd" id="27b811f2edqfd" title="" class="xref">请求参数</a>和<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="d3de9a84edcbx" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>，调用<code data-tag="code" id="efda9b7eb61ar" class="code">call</code>方法进行合成并通过<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="b7ffdc3dfaubo" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="5c03f0c244bu5" class="code">onEvent</code>方法实时获取合成结果。</p><p id="671814d69eelw">发送的文本长度不得超过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>2000<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符（详情请参见<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="7bbe107347siu" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="e738b7047anc5" class="code">call</code>方法）。</p><div type="important" id="950d65a6b8d9a" docid="5503579" is-conref="true" class="note note-important"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note important"></i><strong>重要 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><p id="75e6048b1a46f">每次调用<code data-tag="code" id="b59db2676a478" class="code">call</code>方法前，需要重新初始化<code data-tag="code" id="3e176386c123r" class="code">SpeechSynthesizer</code>实例。</p></div></div>
    <section class="collapse" id="50518ffbc2b5w">
      <div class="expandable-title-bold">
        <span class="title"><p id="43c478789e28e" data-tag="expandable-title" class="expandable-title"><b>点击查看完整示例</b></p></span>
        <i class="icon help-iconfont help-icon-zhankai1 smallFont"></i>
      </div>
      <div class="expandable-content">
        <p id="3e711b9a3da2n">以下示例，展示如何使用同步接口调用语音大模型<span class="help-letter-space"></span>CosyVoice<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的音色“龙小淳（longxiaochun）”，将文案“今天天气怎么样”合成采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>22050Hz，音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>MP3<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的音频。</p>
    <div class="help-code-block">
      <div class="code-tools">
        <div class="left-tools">
        </div>
        <div class="right-tools">
          <i class="theme-switch-btn help-iconfont help-icon-baitian" title="更改代码主题"></i>
      <i class="copy-btn help-iconfont help-icon-fuzhi" title="复制代码"></i>
        </div>
      </div>
      <pre code-type="xCode" id="5edf1ae1d25p2" data-tag="codeblock" outputclass="language-java" class="pre codeblock language-java"><code data-highlighted="yes" class="hljs language-java"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.tts.SpeechSynthesisResult;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesisParam;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesizer;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.common.ResultCallback;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.time.LocalDateTime;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;

<span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">TimeUtils</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">final</span> <span class="hljs-type">DateTimeFormatter</span> <span class="hljs-variable">formatter</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span>
            DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern(<span class="hljs-string">"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss.SSS"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> String <span class="hljs-title function_">getTimestamp</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> LocalDateTime.now().format(formatter);
    }
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Main</span> {
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 模型</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">model</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"cosyvoice-v2"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-comment">// 音色</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">voice</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"longxiaochun_v2"</span>;

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">streamAudioDataToSpeaker</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
        <span class="hljs-type">CountDownLatch</span> <span class="hljs-variable">latch</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">CountDownLatch</span>(<span class="hljs-number">1</span>);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 实现回调接口ResultCallback</span>
        ResultCallback&lt;SpeechSynthesisResult&gt; callback = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ResultCallback</span>&lt;SpeechSynthesisResult&gt;() {
            <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onEvent</span><span class="hljs-params">(SpeechSynthesisResult result)</span> {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// System.out.println("收到消息: " + result);</span>
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (result.getAudioFrame() != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// 此处实现保存音频数据到本地的逻辑</span>
                    System.out.println(TimeUtils.getTimestamp() + <span class="hljs-string">" 收到音频"</span>);
                }
            }

            <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onComplete</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
                System.out.println(TimeUtils.getTimestamp() + <span class="hljs-string">" 收到Complete，语音合成结束"</span>);
                latch.countDown();
            }

            <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onError</span><span class="hljs-params">(Exception e)</span> {
                System.out.println(<span class="hljs-string">"出现异常："</span> + e.toString());
                latch.countDown();
            }
        };

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 请求参数</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesisParam</span> <span class="hljs-variable">param</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span>
                SpeechSynthesisParam.builder()
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// 若没有将API Key配置到环境变量中，需将下面这行代码注释放开，并将your-api-key替换为自己的API Key</span>
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// .apiKey("your-api-key")</span>
                        .model(model) <span class="hljs-comment">// 模型</span>
                        .voice(voice) <span class="hljs-comment">// 音色</span>
                        .build();
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 第二个参数“callback”传入回调即启用异步模式</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesizer</span> <span class="hljs-variable">synthesizer</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">SpeechSynthesizer</span>(param, callback);
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 非阻塞调用，立即返回null（实际结果通过回调接口异步传递），在回调接口的onEvent方法中实时获取二进制音频</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
            synthesizer.call(<span class="hljs-string">"今天天气怎么样？"</span>);
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 等待合成完成</span>
            latch.await();
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 等待播放线程全部播放完</span>
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception e) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RuntimeException</span>(e);
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">finally</span> {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 任务结束后关闭websocket连接</span>
            synthesizer.getDuplexApi().close(<span class="hljs-number">1000</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"bye"</span>);
        }
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 首次发送文本时需建立 WebSocket 连接，因此首包延迟会包含连接建立的耗时</span>
        System.out.println(
                <span class="hljs-string">"[Metric] requestId为："</span>
                        + synthesizer.getLastRequestId()
                        + <span class="hljs-string">"，首包延迟（毫秒）为："</span>
                        + synthesizer.getFirstPackageDelay());
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">(String[] args)</span> {
        streamAudioDataToSpeaker();
        System.exit(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    }
}</code></pre>
    </div>

  </section><section id="e532d85370umz" class="section"><h3 id="ba023aacfbr84"><b>流式调用</b></h3><p id="27312c5342g9m" data-spm-anchor-id="a2c4g.11186623.0.i1.54537447HdUyhP">分多次提交文本，通过注册<code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="47f4bc767fnpx">ResultCallback</code>回调，逐帧接收实时语音分段数据。</p><div id="df00a794d7gip" type="note" class="note note-note"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note note"></i><strong>说明 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><ul id="55f09f6e69753"><li id="143c964a15a61"><p id="1c2af65a3ap1k">流式输入时可多次调用<code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="33d1277d3ahcm">streamingCall</code>按顺序提交文本片段。服务端接收文本片段后自动进行分句：</p><ul id="b75b412c3b22z"><li id="4cfb50d785uzj"><p id="3377a7e7cdfp2">完整语句立即合成</p></li><li id="9a7ce69391fkd"><p id="58525c1650frg">不完整语句缓存至完整后合成</p></li></ul><p id="f889e58ed0fjo">调用 <code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="d13282ac804my">streamingComplete</code> 时，服务端会强制合成所有已接收但未处理的文本片段（包括未完成的句子）。</p></li><li id="52eaf219519cx"><p id="5425b2e986ptk">发送文本片段的间隔不得超过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>23<span class="help-letter-space"></span>秒，否则触发“request timeout after 23 seconds”异常。</p><p id="fbfb0b3f86jp6">若无待发送文本，需及时调用 <code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="db56f6f350pne">streamingComplete</code>结束任务。</p><blockquote id="f0b4d20273zw2" ind="{&quot;left&quot;:32}">服务端强制设定<span class="help-letter-space"></span>23<span class="help-letter-space"></span>秒超时机制，客户端无法修改该配置。</blockquote></li></ul></div></div><hetu type="flowchart" id="8feb91150cqfk" versionid="CAEQVRiBgICHxPGhrBkiIGE3ZTVmMzY0YzI3NzQxYTFiYWE2MmU2NTBhMDgzZGM1" uuid="4709861_20241015153444.149" hetuid="8b05cfed-2017-4ede-af17-20e71960b705"><img src="https://help-static-aliyun-doc.aliyuncs.com/assets/img/zh-CN/9516678571/CAEQVRiBgICHxPGhrBkiIGE3ZTVmMzY0YzI3NzQxYTFiYWE2MmU2NTBhMDgzZGM14709861_20241015153444.149.svg" alt="image" class="image break flowchart hetu" loading="lazy"></hetu><ol id="e8b3793aa5ee7"><li id="a3b86c01bc8ny"><p id="92fda5404ceg7">实例化<span class="help-letter-space"></span>SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</p><p id="116fcfb358enn">实例化<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="c3f5db172b1ym" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>绑定<a href="#a96bfa6340jdd" id="cc8a615fa3hjj" title="" class="xref">请求参数</a>和<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="6a9f1e341d11u" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>。</p></li><li id="712d212f1aqfc"><p id="e0aa0dc3dd8ex">流式传输</p><p id="ce8b5bd472psk">多次调用<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="8c943e3882nyt" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="4f9fc4a324x0p" class="code">streamingCall</code>方法分片提交待合成文本，将待合成文本分段发送至服务端。</p><p id="7bbde7e15ehv9">在发送文本的过程中，服务端会通过<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="41a54c24578r8" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="560fb9ec012ym" class="code">onEvent</code>方法，将合成结果实时返回给客户端。</p><p id="cbee74727bzre">每次调用<code data-tag="code" id="6db474a1ecbao" class="code">streamingCall</code>方法发送的文本片段（即<code data-tag="code" id="26351d512bp7d" class="code">text</code>）长度不得超过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>2000<span class="help-letter-space"></span>字符，累计发送的文本总长度不得超过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>20<span class="help-letter-space"></span>万字符。</p></li><li id="f034d1f9f84ae"><p id="2dbc242aacgjk">结束处理</p><p id="75ac5a99a5ngb">调用<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="9fd2a684c52iq" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="a9bf746712idr" class="code">streamingComplete</code>方法结束语音合成。</p><p id="c30257a41dwup">该方法会阻塞当前线程，直到<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="7b87c9bcbdbzv" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="ff7a998b0fqq0" class="code">onComplete</code>或者<code data-tag="code" id="d922691fd8724" class="code">onError</code>回调触发后才会释放线程阻塞。</p><p id="2e872e38138uf">请务必确保调用该方法，否则可能会导致结尾部分的文本无法成功转换为语音。</p></li></ol>
    <section class="collapse" id="4ba0598f96x9y">

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Main</span> {

            <span class="hljs-string">"可以将输入的文本"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"合成为语音二进制数据，"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"相比于非流式语音合成，"</span>,

            <span class="hljs-string">"可以听到接近同步的语音输出，"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"极大地提升了交互体验，"</span>,

    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">model</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"cosyvoice-v2"</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 模型</span>
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">voice</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"longxiaochun_v2"</span>; <span class="hljs-comment">// 音色</span>

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">streamAudioDataToSpeaker</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 配置回调函数</span>
        ResultCallback&lt;SpeechSynthesisResult&gt; callback = <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">ResultCallback</span>&lt;SpeechSynthesisResult&gt;() {
            <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onEvent</span><span class="hljs-params">(SpeechSynthesisResult result)</span> {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// System.out.println("收到消息: " + result);</span>
                <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (result.getAudioFrame() != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {
                    <span class="hljs-comment">// 此处实现处理音频数据的逻辑</span>
                    System.out.println(TimeUtils.getTimestamp() + <span class="hljs-string">" 收到音频"</span>);
                }
            }

            <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onComplete</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
                System.out.println(TimeUtils.getTimestamp() + <span class="hljs-string">" 收到Complete，语音合成结束"</span>);
            }

            <span class="hljs-meta">@Override</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">onError</span><span class="hljs-params">(Exception e)</span> {
                System.out.println(<span class="hljs-string">"出现异常："</span> + e.toString());
            }
        };

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 请求参数</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesisParam</span> <span class="hljs-variable">param</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span>
                SpeechSynthesisParam.builder()
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// 若没有将API Key配置到环境变量中，需将下面这行代码注释放开，并将your-api-key替换为自己的API Key</span>
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// .apiKey("your-api-key")</span>
                        .model(model)
                        .voice(voice)
                        .format(SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 带Callback的call方法将不会阻塞当前线程</span>
        <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (String text : textArray) {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// 发送文本片段，在回调接口的onEvent方法中实时获取二进制音频</span>
                synthesizer.streamingCall(text);
            }
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 等待结束流式语音合成</span>
            synthesizer.streamingComplete();
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (Exception e) {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RuntimeException</span>(e);
        } <span class="hljs-keyword">finally</span> {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// 任务结束关闭websocket连接</span>
            synthesizer.getDuplexApi().close(<span class="hljs-number">1000</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"bye"</span>);
        }

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 首次发送文本时需建立 WebSocket 连接，因此首包延迟会包含连接建立的耗时</span>
        System.out.println(
                <span class="hljs-string">"[Metric] requestId为："</span>
                        + synthesizer.getLastRequestId()
                        + <span class="hljs-string">"，首包延迟（毫秒）为："</span>
                        + synthesizer.getFirstPackageDelay());
    }

        streamAudioDataToSpeaker();
        System.exit(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    }

  </section><section id="44054c97d839u" class="section"><h3 id="b0f81fef83ojo"><b>通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>调用</b></h3><p id="6c546d5108whs">Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>是一个用于工作流和业务流程管理的开源框架，它基于<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Apache 2.0<span class="help-letter-space"></span>许可证发布。关于<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的使用，请参见<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a class="" href="http://reactivex.io/RxJava/2.x/javadoc/" id="6c900add2fo4y">Flowable API<span class="help-letter-space"></span>详情</a>。</p><p id="36759facfadie">使用<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>前需确保已集成<span class="help-letter-space"></span>RxJava<span class="help-letter-space"></span>库，并了解响应式编程基础概念。</p><section id="f1bbd2dc6apse" data-tag="tabbed-content-box" outputclass="tabbed-content-box" class="tabbed-content-box section"><div class="tab-box"><div class="tab-item-container"><div class="tab-item selected-tab-item" id="ce0a5e1aeanhn">非流式调用</div><div class="tab-item" id="8c9c50ec8aw6b">流式调用</div></div><div class="tab-box-button" style="visibility: hidden;">
  <div class="left deactivateBtn"><i class="help-iconfont help-icon-zhankai1"></i></div>
  <div class="right"><i class="help-iconfont help-icon-zhankai1"></i></div>
  </div></div><section id="7803ca3638fwy" class="section" style="display: block;"><p id="8f1aeb0145fcu">以下示例展示了通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>对象的<code data-tag="code" id="52af6e6ff2z7r" class="code">blockingForEach</code>接口，阻塞式地获取每次流式返回的<code data-tag="code" id="bf014eee5c069" class="code">SpeechSynthesisResult</code>类型数据。</p><p id="7f20a5ec22bay">您也可以在<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的所有流式数据返回完成后，通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="b64d08f5d2ycr" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="5590c197aerxv" class="code">getAudioData</code>来获取完整的合成结果。</p>

        synthesizer.callAsFlowable(<span class="hljs-string">"今天天气怎么样?"</span>).blockingForEach(result -&gt; {
            <span class="hljs-comment">// System.out.println("收到消息: " + result);</span>
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (result.getAudioFrame() != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {

        System.exit(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);

  </section><section id="b0fe97c84eq2u" class="section"><p id="cd804f904bs3l">以下示例展示了通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>对象作为输入参数，输入文本流。并通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>对象作为返回值，利用的<code data-tag="code" id="70d805d2bcmob" class="code">blockingForEach</code>接口，阻塞式地获取每次流式返回的<code data-tag="code" id="d3e7f623535iz" class="code">SpeechSynthesisResult</code>类型数据。</p><p id="6d1082c03e4wy">您也可以在<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的所有流式数据返回完成后，通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="3426b54829a9h" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="d51f9f8d29grm" class="code">getAudioData</code>来获取完整的合成结果。</p>
    <section class="collapse" id="05bf05adf9e1g">
      <div class="expandable-title-bold">
        <span class="title"><p id="985bb89800zwl" data-tag="expandable-title" class="expandable-title"><b>点击查看完整示例</b></p></span>
        <i class="icon help-iconfont help-icon-zhankai1 smallFont"></i>

      <pre code-type="xCode" id="95c492efdazm2" data-tag="codeblock" outputclass="language-java" class="pre codeblock language-java"><code data-highlighted="yes" class="hljs language-java"><span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesisParam;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesizer;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> com.alibaba.dashscope.exception.NoApiKeyException;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> io.reactivex.BackpressureStrategy;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> io.reactivex.Flowable;

<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.time.LocalDateTime;
<span class="hljs-keyword">import</span> java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;

<span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">TimeUtils</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">final</span> <span class="hljs-type">DateTimeFormatter</span> <span class="hljs-variable">formatter</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span>
            DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern(<span class="hljs-string">"yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss.SSS"</span>);

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> String <span class="hljs-title function_">getTimestamp</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> {
        <span class="hljs-keyword">return</span> LocalDateTime.now().format(formatter);
    }
}

<span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">class</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Main</span> {
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> String[] textArray = {<span class="hljs-string">"流式文本语音合成SDK，"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-string">"可以将输入的文本"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"合成为语音二进制数据，"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"相比于非流式语音合成，"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-string">"流式合成的优势在于实时性"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"更强。用户在输入文本的同时"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-string">"可以听到接近同步的语音输出，"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"极大地提升了交互体验，"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-string">"减少了用户等待时间。"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"适用于调用大规模"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"语言模型（LLM），以"</span>,
            <span class="hljs-string">"流式输入文本的方式"</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"进行语音合成的场景。"</span>};
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">model</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"cosyvoice-v2"</span>;
    <span class="hljs-keyword">private</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-type">String</span> <span class="hljs-variable">voice</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-string">"longxiaochun_v2"</span>;

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">streamAudioDataToSpeaker</span><span class="hljs-params">()</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">throws</span> NoApiKeyException {
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 模拟流式输入</span>
        Flowable&lt;String&gt; textSource = Flowable.create(emitter -&gt; {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">Thread</span>(() -&gt; {
                <span class="hljs-keyword">for</span> (<span class="hljs-type">int</span> <span class="hljs-variable">i</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-number">0</span>; i &lt; textArray.length; i++) {
                    emitter.onNext(textArray[i]);
                    <span class="hljs-keyword">try</span> {
                        Thread.sleep(<span class="hljs-number">1000</span>);
                    } <span class="hljs-keyword">catch</span> (InterruptedException e) {
                        <span class="hljs-keyword">throw</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">RuntimeException</span>(e);
                    }
                }
                emitter.onComplete();
            }).start();
        }, BackpressureStrategy.BUFFER);

        <span class="hljs-comment">// 请求参数</span>
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesisParam</span> <span class="hljs-variable">param</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span>
                SpeechSynthesisParam.builder()
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// 若没有将API Key配置到环境变量中，需将下面这行代码注释放开，并将apiKey替换为自己的API Key</span>
                        <span class="hljs-comment">// .apiKey("yourApikey")</span>
                        .model(model) <span class="hljs-comment">// 模型</span>
                        .voice(voice) <span class="hljs-comment">// 音色</span>
                        .build();
        <span class="hljs-type">SpeechSynthesizer</span> <span class="hljs-variable">synthesizer</span> <span class="hljs-operator">=</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">new</span> <span class="hljs-title class_">SpeechSynthesizer</span>(param, <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>);
        synthesizer.streamingCallAsFlowable(textSource).blockingForEach(result -&gt; {
            <span class="hljs-keyword">if</span> (result.getAudioFrame() != <span class="hljs-literal">null</span>) {
                <span class="hljs-comment">// 此处实现播放音频的逻辑</span>
                System.out.println(
                        TimeUtils.getTimestamp() +
                                <span class="hljs-string">" 二进制音频大小为："</span> + result.getAudioFrame().capacity());
            }
        });
        synthesizer.getDuplexApi().close(<span class="hljs-number">1000</span>, <span class="hljs-string">"bye"</span>);
        <span class="hljs-comment">// 首次发送文本时需建立 WebSocket 连接，因此首包延迟会包含连接建立的耗时</span>
        System.out.println(
                <span class="hljs-string">"[Metric] requestId为："</span>
                        + synthesizer.getLastRequestId()
                        + <span class="hljs-string">"，首包延迟（毫秒）为："</span>
                        + synthesizer.getFirstPackageDelay());
    }

    <span class="hljs-keyword">public</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">static</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">void</span> <span class="hljs-title function_">main</span><span class="hljs-params">(String[] args)</span> <span class="hljs-keyword">throws</span> NoApiKeyException {
        streamAudioDataToSpeaker();
        System.exit(<span class="hljs-number">0</span>);
    }
}</code></pre>
    </div>

      </div>
    </section>
  </section></section></section><section id="3364ce308epvw" class="section"><h3 id="93d37d8ec4vw8"><b>高并发调用</b></h3><p id="31712623fb6ya">在<span class="help-letter-space"></span>DashScope Java SDK<span class="help-letter-space"></span>中，采用了<span class="help-letter-space"></span>OkHttp3<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的连接池技术，以减少重复建立连接的开销。详情请参见<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/high-concurrency-scenarios" id="68e3a0c545r3p" title="" class="xref">高并发场景</a>。</p></section></section><section id="2e9a9a89aclc8" class="section"><h2 id="a96bfa6340jdd"><b>请求参数</b></h2><p id="b2dc1353c6epb">通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>SpeechSynthesisParam<span class="help-letter-space"></span>的链式方法配置模型、音色等参数。配置完成的参数对象传入<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="#adcb5e9bddbyq" id="441b08f8abrkr" title="" class="xref">SpeechSynthesizer<span class="help-letter-space"></span>类</a>的构造函数中使用。</p>
    <section class="collapse" id="fcc28950f223c">

id="1d1fce370c10j"><b>是否必须</b></p></span></td><td id="9a84a971d73oq" rowspan="1" style="background-color:#e5e5e5;vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><span><p id="b16cfea131yxu"><b>说明</b></p></span></td></tr></thead></table><table id="3054e12d074om" tablewidth="100" tablecolswidth="13.59 10.92 11.15 14.17 50.17" autofit="true" class="table"><colgroup colwidth="0.68*" style="width:13.59%"></colgroup><colgroup colwidth="0.55*" style="width:10.92%"></colgroup><colgroup colwidth="0.56*" style="width:11.15%"></colgroup><colgroup colwidth="0.71*" style="width:14.17%"></colgroup><colgroup colwidth="2.51*" style="width:50.17%"></colgroup><tbody class="tbody"><tr id="9963b484592zh"><td id="3966cdd7e8285" rowspan="1" style="background-color:#e5e5e5;vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="11def0259fmb7"><b>参数</b></p></td><td id="161ca2ab20fw6" rowspan="1" style="background-color:#e5e5e5;vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="d4a5ad520d4kg"><b>类型</b></p></td><td id="ebc812e947q3n" rowspan="1" style="background-color:#e5e5e5;vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="f6b43e25c7n5k"><b>默认值</b></p></td><td id="aacfeac11a38v" rowspan="1" style="background-color:#e5e5e5;vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="1d1fce370c10j"><b>是否必须</b></p></td><td id="9a84a971d73oq" rowspan="1" style="background-color:#e5e5e5;vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="b16cfea131yxu"><b>说明</b></p></td></tr><tr id="b048e0d3fbli8"><td id="1f8d7721b1ix4" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="17998ee269w1m">model</p></td><td id="d25465017882z" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="175bb1286fe6e">String</p></td><td id="512bf472b98u8" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="5acd14c176t90">-</p></td><td id="6136a58de4nuu" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="5707270effozc">是</p></td><td id="2cd1fdc5b3yup" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><section id="7c0fb3319bgvu" class="section"><p id="05964ed0b4fl2">指定模型。</p><p id="c8fd37e59a2v6">不同版本的模型编码方式一致，但使用时须确保模型（<code data-tag="code" id="6c373e76ed196" class="code">model</code>）与音色（<code data-tag="code" id="eb99082c29bw9" class="code">voice</code>）匹配：每个版本的模型只能使用本版本的默认音色或专属音色。</p></section></td></tr><tr id="8bfba225315ew"><td id="9cee27e00f6t2" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="30754597c7xjc">voice</p></td><td id="cd1c210b4c0k9" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="88cb77a200p0v">String</p></td><td id="5733a3b2a4jol" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="6b71a2cff3w4w">-</p></td><td id="81ca74e19ehlk" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="d5d0f90e4a0e0">是</p></td><td id="e8ba2c7f94oa7" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><section id="e0d9c96cfbwi4" class="section"><p id="3859a94dcaya7">指定语音合成所使用的音色。</p><p jc="left" uuid="megum80xsc7rl99ho2" id="487254cc225qa" style="text-align:left">支持默认音色和专属音色：</p><ul id="7c9d3776990yp"><li id="80660904cau68"><p jc="left" uuid="megumclddlf9fdjp6wc" id="d282607a26vzk" style="text-align:left"><b>默认音色</b>：参见<b>音色列表</b>章节。</p></li><li id="f100d3f789zz6"><p id="a63b34940c7dr"><b>专属音色</b>：通过<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/voice-replica-1/" id="ca5e36794ci9s" title="" class="xref">声音复刻</a>功能定制。使用复刻音色时，请确保声音复刻与语音合成使用同一账号。详细操作步骤请参见<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/cosyvoice-clone-api#da30eeebc4uwk" id="2ac6d77091jfs" title="" class="xref">语音合成</a>。</p></li></ul><section id="ca1192d32cerk" class="section"><p id="5242960d06p2h"><b>⚠️ 使用声音复刻系列模型合成语音时，仅能使用该模型复刻生成的专属音色，不能使用默认音色。</b></p><p id="5433b8a58dejt"><b>⚠️ 使用专属音色合成语音时，语音合成模型（</b><code data-tag="code" id="e8098d7f92r7x" class="code"><b>model</b></code><b>）必须与声音复刻模型（</b><code data-tag="code" id="6384c6e6fcgby" class="code"><b>target_model</b></code><b>）相同。</b></p></section></section></td></tr><tr id="d9529985caf75"><td id="95d349d6efic1" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="b06a674d114vc">format</p></td><td id="5ff66930c4yop" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="637cf41f262t6">enum</p></td><td id="2b6afc1c937ia" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="d168284b2dft3">因音色而异</p></td><td id="5d3b9b8bf5le0" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="612cb77de3y28">否</p></td><td id="9c39f2d8a8zxi" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p jc="left" id="a261b4814bt38" style="text-align:left">指定音频编码格式及采样率。</p><p id="1d0cab4141iws">若未指定<code data-tag="code" id="c9deaf8a71ow9" class="code">format</code>，则合成音频采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>22.05kHz，格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3。</p><div type="note" id="313dc68419lya" docid="5282227" is-conref="true" class="note note-note"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note note"></i><strong>说明 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><p jc="left" uuid="lx1krquz2bg2hqcl7ux" id="61cfbba8534ym" style="text-align:left">默认采样率代表当前音色的最佳采样率，缺省条件下默认按照该采样率输出，同时支持降采样或升采样。</p></div></div><p id="90c5b57fa7oy1">可指定的音频编码格式及采样率如下：</p><ul id="21bb699f69bgm"><li id="07a759002arz9"><p id="e980fcf44cf3k">所有模型均支持的音频编码格式及采样率：</p><ul id="aa2612fbb7zox"><li id="8eb5de45b2q59"><p id="a91befc2b30co">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.WAV_8000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>wav，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>8kHz</p></li><li id="75d22dab77hfd"><p id="8ba697e0115kb">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.WAV_16000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>wav，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kHz</p></li><li id="9210b31e9dulm"><p id="afbab3aa8d7ua">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.WAV_22050HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>wav，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>22.05kHz</p></li><li id="2a2f7fce82vlq"><p id="07185fe83dcu3">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.WAV_24000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>wav，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>24kHz</p></li><li id="cc6777f202j18"><p id="a5dade9225m6m">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.WAV_44100HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>wav，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>44.1kHz</p></li><li id="42e19c59d3toh"><p id="9f74335c84z8e">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.WAV_48000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>wav，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>48kHz</p></li><li id="f5ce915229uyv"><p id="e2403f0c24ny3">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.MP3_8000HZ_MONO_128KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>8kHz</p></li><li id="674b9adbc4gq0"><p id="f013140b5cznx">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.MP3_16000HZ_MONO_128KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kHz</p></li><li id="113addde5bkfj"><p id="4d75d178bbg85">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.MP3_22050HZ_MONO_256KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>22.05kHz</p></li><li id="ee4bff4ea1x13"><p id="e113c1bd52e3t">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.MP3_24000HZ_MONO_256KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>24kHz</p></li><li id="54babcc9a6x8k"><p id="347fe946ebebp">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.MP3_44100HZ_MONO_256KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>44.1kHz</p></li><li id="d3192cf79bs6a"><p id="8c65d28dac3l5">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.MP3_48000HZ_MONO_256KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>mp3，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>48kHz</p></li><li id="0e1d9ec523uee"><p id="0f45f75394sub">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.PCM_8000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>pcm，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>8kHz</p></li><li id="8d7ba4cbb0mty"><p id="5c8f65c244c4c">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.PCM_16000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>pcm，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kHz</p></li><li id="03c0e700f6clb"><p id="2f4f2e1f31uqr">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.PCM_22050HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>pcm，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>22.05kHz</p></li><li id="ba8334d95ce38"><p id="cb7b568fec0lb">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.PCM_24000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>pcm，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>24kHz</p></li><li id="20340dc76170b"><p id="e0cf6459a1ykp">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.PCM_44100HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>pcm，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>44.1kHz</p></li><li id="157167924avy8"><p id="b4230ec0a3knh">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.PCM_48000HZ_MONO_16BIT，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>pcm，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>48kHz</p></li></ul></li><li id="7ebda388adnv9"><p id="8dbd08d083i4j"><span data-tag="ph" id="0330147eb3bp3" props="china" data-cond-props="china" class="ph">除<code data-tag="code" id="29607fd36buzh" class="code">cosyvoice-v1</code>外，其他模型支持的音频编码格式及采样率：</span></p><p id="968066f430z38">音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus<span class="help-letter-space"></span>时，支持通过<code data-tag="code" id="d5462bf3f9hq4" class="code">bit_rate</code>参数调整码率。仅对<span class="help-letter-space"></span>2.21.0<span class="help-letter-space"></span>及之后版本的<span class="help-letter-space"></span>DashScope<span class="help-letter-space"></span>适用。</p><ul id="0b1ad17b93rco"><li id="187ae52af9eod"><p id="42be893c177v5">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_8KHZ_MONO_32KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>8kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>32kbps</p></li><li id="6365ec420a637"><p id="3bca1a7af8b26">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_16KHZ_MONO_16KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kbps</p></li><li id="1da59707c7c2p"><p id="65db88f131d0q">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_16KHZ_MONO_32KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>32kbps</p></li><li id="9864948b4fjw0"><p id="b850d1dd78a7n">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_16KHZ_MONO_64KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>64kbps</p></li><li id="5c6f77e5a0pif"><p id="9af574fff19lr">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_24KHZ_MONO_16KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>24kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kbps</p></li><li id="98e91d8715n0o"><p id="c4dfe281bdjjx">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_24KHZ_MONO_32KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>24kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>32kbps</p></li><li id="b2f605990f67m"><p id="874e3d0330as7">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_24KHZ_MONO_64KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>24kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>64kbps</p></li><li id="7eae98b17ebf9"><p id="d85d1f2024gjt">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_48KHZ_MONO_16KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>48kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>16kbps</p></li><li id="ed48bfc7036b4"><p id="34af941920ptv">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_48KHZ_MONO_32KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>48kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>32kbps</p></li><li id="2ba0a191d19xk"><p id="cb16266cf80vv">SpeechSynthesisAudioFormat.OGG_OPUS_48KHZ_MONO_64KBPS，代表音频格式为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus，采样率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>48kHz，码率为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>64kbps</p></li></ul></li></ul></td></tr><tr id="5d3f353037giv"><td id="84b108bdd0i3h" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="fb87f7ac44m6c">volume</p></td><td id="efa1ca6bee0ml" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="a77044d823hao">int</p></td><td id="c3b8614cebacg" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="e0b4473730t27">50</p></td><td id="773fb286e90qi" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="6e61c316fcws2">否</p></td><td id="04cade58465g7" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p jc="left" uuid="lwrm2u4ylu337643m3" id="4bab1d1d3b4s3" style="text-align:left">指定音量，取值范围：0~100。</p></td></tr><tr id="42510facaa3ks"><td id="62bbbda4d6qle" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="07ed6b2407rfg">speechRate</p></td><td id="8e8a24c2e8280" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="79c5800b050ub">float</p></td><td id="88afdba1ebczn" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="270c2b24cfkiu">1.0</p></td><td id="7cb4a90a5bsx8" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="a8a3d726a0wpe">否</p></td><td id="5738c4b879tpo" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p jc="left" id="6533a1b58adc4" style="text-align:left">指定语速，取值范围：0.5~2。</p><ul id="b53b8935e4702"><li id="7e856a54d9yha"><p id="55078e9df2m6u">0.5：表示默认语速的<span class="help-letter-space"></span>0.5<span class="help-letter-space"></span>倍速。</p></li><li id="50c2e9efcdes5"><p id="688fde1859hu1">1：表示默认语速。默认语速是指模型默认输出的合成语速，语速会因音色不同而略有不同。约每秒钟<span class="help-letter-space"></span>4<span class="help-letter-space"></span>个字。</p></li><li id="64dc79a246z6d"><p id="9afdfeb4134xc">2：表示默认语速的<span class="help-letter-space"></span>2<span class="help-letter-space"></span>倍速。</p></li></ul></td></tr><tr id="2ff5f29d4c5t1"><td id="048b16e8ddtqo" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="f89792cdeb2bu">pitchRate</p></td><td id="24db1fec1bvfr" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="011786bb256a1">float</p></td><td id="02ca08447bfxs" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="86d6b699e5p1b">1.0</p></td><td id="2134566c7ctbi" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="420891e9a6qmk">否</p></td><td id="242fc18b76q2j" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="e71d6e97b8gp6">指定语调，取值范围：0.5~2。</p></td></tr><tr id="5aa3f78aa6sai"><td id="92eb51e38dvgs" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="84b8d6815al66">bit_rate</p></td><td id="c6d322be8af34" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="81afe4ecf8mho">int</p></td><td id="ed329432c790n" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="63da3e2a06x7o">32</p></td><td id="72dbaa1d41q1u" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="664038a1c9jhz">否</p></td><td id="792d1ddf1btte" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><section id="9100414c986td" class="section"><p id="88569c0360ulf">指定音频的<a class="" href="https://opus-codec.org/" id="4580d6994bk4k">码率</a>，取值范围：6~510kbps。</p><p id="d1c1f152a97vf">码率越大，音质越好，音频文件体积越大。</p><p id="a83974f34cwjs">仅在音频格式（<code data-tag="code" id="87ea5d2599jrd" class="code">format</code>）为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>opus<span class="help-letter-space"></span>时可用。</p><p id="6ca96d3d653t2"><span data-tag="ph" id="d0db33ae842wk" props="china" data-cond-props="china" class="ph"><code data-tag="code" id="f0b81b3561y5y" class="code">cosyvoice-v1</code>模型不支持该参数。</span></p></section><div type="note" id="2616a0950bka2" class="note note-note"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note note"></i><strong>说明 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><p jc="left" id="c5993c3cc7yvx" style="text-align:left"><code data-tag="code" id="d17bd60ab7ymr" class="code">bit_rate</code>需要通过<code data-tag="code" id="cf8e97616fxgi" class="code">SpeechSynthesisParam</code>实例的<code data-tag="code" id="fa17f3f9c8fm3" class="code">parameter</code>方法或者<code data-tag="code" id="cc458fefefj51" class="code">parameters</code>方法进行设置：</p><section id="a181d0694a70h" data-tag="tabbed-content-box" outputclass="tabbed-content-box" class="tabbed-content-box section"><div class="tab-box"><div class="tab-item-container"><div class="tab-item selected-tab-item" colspan="1"><p id="c416e137cd3ln">bool</p></td><td id="fe5dc288af2cj" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="9c00f0856fjta">false</p></td><td id="5bbbfa27f98sp" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="97c576b6f7qxt">否</p></td><td id="7864adfb91dj0" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><section id="8d6debefb6yzp" class="section"><p id="55f2dca543bdg">是否开启字级别时间戳，默认关闭。</p><p id="3749fda9d09fy">仅<span class="help-letter-space"></span>cosyvoice-v2<span class="help-letter-space"></span>支持该功能。</p><blockquote id="fbd451cea2498">时间戳结果仅能通过回调接口获取</blockquote></section></td></tr><tr id="80a232b0d6xmm"><td id="8ba7e255c2zj8" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="ba615171d89e6">seed</p></td><td id="4f96c6d9ffwa8" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="69673dafb263b">int</p></td><td id="add89f035aqng" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="3842ebc932fl9">0</p></td><td id="4b1c885d144vo" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="65c8f7ecc6yxs">否</p></td><td id="05226aff41ryk" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><section id="d89ecd70549ut" class="section"><p id="85dc68d1bc49e">生成时使用的随机数种子，使合成的效果产生变化。默认值<span class="help-letter-space"></span>0。取值范围：0~65535。</p><p id="d5365e1e414vn">仅<span class="help-letter-space"></span>cosyvoice-v3、cosyvoice-v3-plus<span class="help-letter-space"></span>支持该功能。</p></section></td></tr><tr id="db328eca0c5o7"><td id="fe0e518ec2ikk" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="d77ae38d8feck">languageHints</p></td><td id="5eb859bea7l7c" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="a672b1c7f3eyh">List</p></td><td id="d741f204aduob" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="373565dc1a1cp">-</p></td><td id="e14a24c001dmv" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="a51fc86565bwb">否</p></td><td id="319ccfe3e7xzu" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><section id="79f923362eua4" class="section"><p id="14bd363a3dnsa">合成文本语言提示，可选值为&nbsp;<code data-tag="code" class="code react-markdown-blog-code" id="c36a55dc4fzsx">zh</code>（中文）或&nbsp;<code data-tag="code" class="code react-markdown-blog-code" id="0a3dec9619xbv">en</code>（英文），列表中仅第一个语言生效。</p><p id="8775d55cc1gem">仅<span class="help-letter-space"></span>cosyvoice-v3、cosyvoice-v3-plus<span class="help-letter-space"></span>支持该功能。</p><p id="41e31d5860b9x">此设置会影响阿拉伯数字等内容的读法。例如，当合成“123”时，若设置为<code data-tag="code" id="e146044020wat" class="code">zh</code>，则读作“一百二十三”；而<code data-tag="code" id="c64664398ba1m" data-init-id="e146044020wat" class="code">en</code>则会读作“one hundred and twenty-three”。</p><p id="113dde67a758j">如果不设置，系统会根据文本内容自动判断并应用相应的合成规则。</p></section></td></tr><tr id="ee49117818zvx"><td id="b4f1832caappc" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="d91f9ce4b5eex">instruction</p></td><td id="9cb3956ee6w4t" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="f01afbf26b2if">String</p></td><td id="70cbe74ec23fo" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="85c4384754rxl">-</p></td><td id="c9c34c3ce71eq" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="118540a84bng4">否</p></td><td id="c11e3e5e37v3w" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><section id="f9d438e4d4udq" class="section"><p id="579cc2dfbbk7n">设置提示词。</p><p id="448820a1684bn">仅<span class="help-letter-space"></span>cosyvoice-v3、cosyvoice-v3-plus<span class="help-letter-space"></span>支持该功能。</p><p id="8a5c867781w95">目前仅支持设置情感。</p><p id="8fdd4ab13egwg">格式：“<code data-tag="code" id="76727db0d7l1a" class="code">你说话的情感是&lt;情感值&gt;。</code>”（注意，结尾一定不要遗漏句号）。</p><p id="94cb11d0431mb">支持的情感值：<code data-tag="code" id="94d239647etxl" class="code">neutral</code>、<code data-tag="code" id="83edf1f0a0rur" class="code">fearful</code>、<code data-tag="code" id="7b932da67df6l" class="code">angry</code>、<code data-tag="code" id="96241d15227ys" class="code">sad</code>、<code data-tag="code" id="98ceb5e5b9oxo" class="code">surprised</code>、<code data-tag="code" id="3f3b7935ccn6o" class="code">happy</code>、<code data-tag="code" id="e2829ef742lmi" class="code">disgusted</code>。</p></section></td></tr><tr id="819f9cf0b298i"><td id="b4868d20d198h" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="8c2f4a61b19le">apiKey</p></td><td id="fc26746bb24y4" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="e3ace76fcd9ny">String</p></td><td id="a2bee73f933xs" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="a5fd3b5c576en">-</p></td><td id="7a025c4579owg" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="6362885bf7k2g">否</p></td><td id="4501548d2cxiv" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="67c45103d1blf">指定用户<span class="help-letter-space"></span>API Key。</p></td></tr></tbody></table></div></section><section id="d83081fd10157" class="section"><h2 id="843fb17087zct"><b>关键接口</b></h2><section id="bc8d131a37dmm" class="section"><h3 id="adcb5e9bddbyq"><code data-tag="code" id="7a09e215a7s77" class="code">SpeechSynthesizer</code>类</h3><p id="bade327ad1x8v"><code data-tag="code" id="fb86f4deeev7h" class="code">SpeechSynthesizer</code>通过“<code data-tag="code" id="fe194fefectud" class="code">import com.alibaba.dashscope.audio.ttsv2.SpeechSynthesizer;</code>”方式引入，提供语音合成的关键接口。</p><div     </td><td id="42c2c2db24b6n" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><ul id="361eb671b121k"><li id="b31bf976dakfg"><p id="f16b107c1df8z"><code data-tag="code" id="c097bf8a52bes" class="code">param</code>：<a href="#a96bfa6340jdd" id="d60b000e81dop" title="" class="xref">请求参数</a></p></li><li id="002a52298csrx"><p id="97835a6ef0olv"><code data-tag="code" id="6651024e9a2f0" class="code">callback</code>：</p><ul id="2cc89e1ad5rvg"><li id="3c0d93f351sdh"><p id="ba4ed0c744wdo"><a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="c5e32eb310it8" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>：流式调用/异步调用</p></li><li id="e98c81aee1kt5"><p id="7a48594466b62"><code data-tag="code" id="8da0a4b615a13" class="code">null</code>：同步调用</p></li></ul></li></ul></td><td id="3d25de4ebc3lm" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="5dec643951u4n"><code data-tag="code" id="3d4f6e3f81njz" class="code">SpeechSynthesizer</code>实例</p></td><td id="d3372b2bfcrkb" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="4b5f3753eak5r">构造函数。</p><ul id="2c8bf15dd50m9"><li id="38b7982d54soo"><p id="0551dcc79e2z0">当您使用<a href="#cc2a504f344s2" id="f8613fd361l1y" title="" class="xref">异步调用</a>或<a href="#ba023aacfbr84" id="4cc40e638a4se" title="" class="xref">流式调用</a>模式时，请将<span class="help-letter-space"></span>callback<span class="help-letter-space"></span>参数设置为<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="9cb6c8031bwku" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>。</p></li><li id="cc3e49f277d8f"><p id="172e47a0d5e5g">当您使用<a href="#82d9324616ifx" id="5418ec0120u2t" title="" class="xref">同步调用</a>或<a href="#b0f81fef83ojo" id="ecfd517d9fpgp" title="" class="xref">通过<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Flowable<span class="help-letter-space"></span>调用</a>模式时，请将<span class="help-letter-space"></span>callback<span class="help-letter-space"></span>参数设为<span class="help-letter-space"></span>null。</p></li></ul></td></tr><tr id="ae63876c37ux4"><td id="06749199a2tjv" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1">

    </td><td id="6a51c296a4o37" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="854b023d8fisn"><code data-tag="code" id="49e2f5a748gpu" class="code">text</code>：待合成文本（UTF-8）</p></td><td id="98b80899f03rh" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p id="c3e2d51bb2x5k"><code data-tag="code" id="457f1b095f3m0" class="code">ByteBuffer</code>或<code data-tag="code" id="d482aaca0a5xm" class="code">null</code></p></td><td id="2b54cc9597dib" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1"><p jc="left" id="c1fac4adfcj3m" style="text-align:left">将整段文本（无论是纯文本还是包含<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/introduction-to-cosyvoice-ssml-markup-language" id="3993cc4de06uh" title="" class="xref">SSML</a><span class="help-letter-space"></span>的文本）转换为语音。</p><p id="f3f65623f01yt">在创建<code data-tag="code" class="code" id="323afcbc874mn">SpeechSynthesizer</code>实例时，存在以下两种情况：</p><ul id="9fd9e20912img"><li id="32502db373rrs"><p jc="left" id="f01a601557d72" style="text-align:left">没有指定<code data-tag="code" class="code" id="80ea7d9399ak3">ResultCallback</code>：<code data-tag="code" class="code" id="7fbc3a5490lgj">call</code>方法会阻塞当前线程直到语音合成完成。使用方法请参见<a href="#82d9324616ifx" id="5b357f32d8a46" title="" class="xref">同步调用</a>。</p></li><li id="b8846d408bhhp"><p id="fb13c5abd5xno">指定了<code data-tag="code" class="code" id="7bd029d2752fq">ResultCallback</code>：<code data-tag="code" class="code" id="663cf07b70g7y">call</code>方法会立刻返回<span class="help-letter-space"></span>null。合成结果通过<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="74ad369d2e9cr" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="2d7a0e16efqx4" class="code">onEvent</code>方法获取。使用方法请参见<a href="#cc2a504f344s2" id="fa4c38b212q56" title="" class="xref">异步调用</a>。</p></li></ul><div type="important" id="8ff6a57c06fck" docid="5503579" is-conref="true" class="note note-important"><div class="note-icon-wrapper"><i class="icon-note note important"></i><strong>重要 </strong></div><div class="noteContentSpan"><p id="75e6048b1a46f">每次调用<code data-tag="code" id="b59db2676a478" class="code">call</code>方法前，需要重新初始化<code data-tag="code" id="3e176386c123r" class="code">SpeechSynthesizer</code>实例。</p></div></div></td></tr><tr id="11839c4ce941u"><td id="63f6ee7c464a4" rowspan="1" style="vertical-align:middle" colspan="1">

    <section class="collapse" id="b14a3dfd7f8n7">

id="8a3258c81d5td">服务器返回二进制音频数据：</p><ul id="363bfcaac054a"><li id="a38c4c4c34eok"><p id="84785b7a4c9he"><a href="#82d9324616ifx" id="6b53ee486ep9d" title="" class="xref">同步调用</a>：对<span id="b2f3b35839ltz" class="code">call</code>方法返回的二进制音频数据进行处理。</p></li><li id="24559523a5vak"><p id="3a674f8bf0zob"><a href="#cc2a504f344s2" id="0b632d5950kn7" title="" class="xref">异步调用</a>或<a href="#ba023aacfbr84" id="1b40c2961dyof" title="" class="xref">流式调用</a>：对<a href="#3639e1cb40mxi" id="014a0bd400ggh" title="" class="xref">回调接口（ResultCallback）</a>的<code data-tag="code" id="08cf04aa57xei" class="code">onEvent</code>方法的参数（<code data-tag="code" id="220797b957lqk" class="code">SpeechSynthesisResult</code>类型）进行处理。</p><p id="eec5791d0e7qg"><code data-tag="code" class="code">Sentence</code>：截止当前，本次请求中计费的句子</p><blockquote id="e6dc7e948cwww">需要开启<code data-tag="code" id="7cb5618b84ned" class="code">enableWordTimestamp</code>字级别时间戳</blockquote></td><td id="6c936d46f5hqb" rowspan="1" colspan="1"><p id="1227e10123wo8">返回<code data-tag="code" id="ae6867e6f3i12" data-init-id="5c479518b4xft" class="code">Sentence</code>或<code data-tag="code" id="c5ba4cbfb1k0s" data-init-id="fe76215188yy5" class="code">null</code>。</p><p id="d6b4c5caa0wge"><code data-tag="code" id="2dcd0c2a76kcv" data-init-id="5c479518b4xft" class="code">Sentence</code>的方法：</p><ul id="9189b9fa61vip"><li id="1b6f227465drh"><p id="cfd8f209f9m0e"><code data-tag="code" id="7812fd7d77nxk" class="code">getIndex</code>：可获取句子编号，从<span class="help-letter-space"></span>0<span class="help-letter-space"></span>开始。</p></li><li id="e3147c5f96kn4"><p id="14c725bc02kji"><code data-tag="code" id="ae837279124v9" class="code">getWords</code>：可获取组成句子的字符数组<code data-tag="code" id="900b6d775e1ia" class="code">List&lt;Word&gt;</code>，请以最后一次收到的<code data-tag="code" id="a72a51eca598w" data-init-id="5c479518b4xft" class="code">Sentence</code>为准。</p></li></ul><p id="b0797a7bb53mf"><code data-tag="code" id="b6326c6d52oq6" class="code">Word</code>方法：</p><ul id="a235aafd4b9mr"><li id="94b55438c8xvz"><p id="b232ca629d1rg"><code data-tag="code" id="a7fc906f72q1t" class="code">getText</code>：获取字的文本。</p></li><li id="171d5a9b85p0l"><p id="201dd1a46cl4e"><code data-tag="code" id="83807556f159o" class="code">getBeginIndex</code>：获取字在句子中的开始位置索引，从 0 开始。</p></li><li id="d8bd2c60f486l"><p id="d56128fbf5n0g"><code data-tag="code" id="c093592434bkk" class="code">getEndIndex</code>：获取字在句子中的结束位置索引，从 1 开始。</p></li><li id="443e9789c56bu"><p id="717ce2e2975b6"><code data-tag="code" id="f2430476f3yue" class="code">getBeginTime</code>：获取字对应音频的开始时间戳，单位为毫秒。</p></li><li id="0d4a0450edhkv"><p id="3710c78bfbaam"><code data-tag="code" id="31ff519770psc" class="code">getEndTime</code>：获取字对应音频的结束时间戳，单位为毫秒。</p></li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table></div></li></ul></section><section id="e68ad1d2f7cwg" class="section"><h2 id="75df3e20f46ro"><b>错误码</b></h2><section id="2ec8aa2a9d2h1" class="section"><p id="c7e14b8892vse">如遇报错问题，请参见<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/error-code" id="b9ab93e4ceo95" title="" class="xref">错误信息</a>进行排查。</p><p id="b57f883e23li4">若问题仍未解决，请加入<a class="" href="https://github.com/aliyun/alibabacloud-bailian-speech-demo" id="03fe55176248m">开发者群</a>反馈遇到的问题，并提供<span class="help-letter-space"></span>Request ID，以便进一步排查问题。</p></section></section><section id="d637ba83805wd" class="section"><h2 id="1f2bb8a423d5l"><b>更多示例</b></h2><p id="b69d8307c6142">更多示例，请参见<span class="help-letter-space"></span><a class="" href="https://github.com/aliyun/alibabacloud-bailian-speech-demo" id="12a036992fial">GitHub</a>。</p></section><section id="95303fd00f0ge" class="section"><h2 id="722dd7ca66a6x"><b>音色列表</b></h2><section id="865debb866wvu" docid="5282227" is-conref="true" class="section"><p id="033e7d0686y2f">当前默认支持的音色如下表所示。若您需要更加个性化的音色，可通过声音复刻功能免费定制专属音色，详情请参见<a href="https://help.aliyun.com/zh/model-studio/cosyvoice-clone-api#b6d3449fb336v" id="b20964e2433uf" title="" class="xref">使用复刻的音色进行语音合成</a>。</p><p id="153167cf84asq">进行语音合成时，<code data-tag="code" class="code blog-code" id="1786fe9dd3fub">model</code>参数必须与所选音色对应，否则调用将失败。</p><p id="23c5a05653v7i">待合成文本（text）应使用与所选音色语种一致的语言，否则可能出现发音错误或不自然</p><section id="eff6f01f84ex3" data-tag="tabbed-content-box" outputclass="tabbed-content-box" class="tabbed-content-box section"><div class="tab-box"><div class="tab-item-container"><div class="tab-item selected-tab-item" id="0c318f66322c8">cosyvoice-v3</div><div class="tab-item" id="dc692b9b51p27">cosyvoice-v2</div><div class="tab-item" id="915a935d871ak">cosyvoice-v1</div></div><div class="tab-box-button"
